CREATE TABLE departments (dept_id INT PRIMARY KEY, dept_name VARCHAR(50), location VARCHAR(100))

CREATE TABLE students (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), age INT, grade VARCHAR(10))

CREATE TABLE teachers (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), subject VARCHAR(50), experience INT)</t><s>show create table departments</s>
